Overview" href="#tool-use-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Roo Code implements a sophisticated tool system that allows AI models to interact with your development environment in a controlled and secure manner. This document explains how tools work, when they're called, and how they're managed.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Concepts</h2><a id="user-content-core-concepts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Concepts" href="#core-concepts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tool Groups</h3><a id="user-content-tool-groups" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tool Groups" href="#tool-groups"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools are organized into logical groups based on their functionality:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Category</th>
<th>Purpose</th>
<th>Tools</th>
<th>Common Use</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>Read Group</strong></td>
<td>File system reading and searching</td>
<td><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/read-file">read_file</a>, <a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/search-files">search_files</a>, <a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/list-files">list_files</a>, <a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/list-code-definition-names">list_code_definition_names</a></td>
<td>Code exploration and analysis</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Edit Group</strong></td>
<td>File system modifications</td>
<td><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/apply-diff">apply_diff</a>, <a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/write-to-file">write_to_file</a></td>
<td>Code changes and file manipulation</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Browser Group</strong></td>
<td>Web automation</td>
<td><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/browser-action">browser_action</a></td>
<td>Web testing and interaction</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Command Group</strong></td>
<td>System command execution</td>
<td><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/execute-command">execute_command</a></td>
<td>Running scripts, building projects</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>MCP Group</strong></td>
<td>External tool integration</td>
<td><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/use-mcp-tool">use_mcp_tool</a>, <a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/access-mcp-resource">access_mcp_resource</a></td>
<td>Specialized functionality through external servers</td>
</tr>

<td><strong>Workflow Group</strong></td>

<td>Context switching and task organization</td>
</tr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Always Available Tools</h3><a id="user-content-always-available-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Always Available Tools" href="#always-available-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Certain tools are accessible regardless of the current mode:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/ask-followup-question">ask_followup_question</a>: Gather additional information from users</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/attempt-completion">attempt_completion</a>: Signal task completion</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/switch-mode">switch_mode</a>: Change operational modes</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/new-task">new_task</a>: Create subtasks</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Available Tools</h2><a id="user-content-available-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Available Tools" href="#available-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Read Tools</h3><a id="user-content-read-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Read Tools" href="#read-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These tools help Roo understand your code and project:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/read-file">read_file</a> - Examines the contents of files</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/search-files">search_files</a> - Finds patterns across multiple files</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/list-files">list_files</a> - Maps your project's file structure</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/list-code-definition-names">list_code_definition_names</a> - Creates a structural map of your code</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Edit Tools</h3><a id="user-content-edit-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Edit Tools" href="#edit-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These tools help Roo make changes to your code:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/apply-diff">apply_diff</a> - Makes precise, surgical changes to your code</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/write-to-file">write_to_file</a> - Creates new files or completely rewrites existing ones</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Workflow Tools</h3><a id="user-content-workflow-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Workflow Tools" href="#workflow-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These tools help manage the conversation and task flow:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/ask-followup-question">ask_followup_question</a> - Gets additional information from you</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/attempt-completion">attempt_completion</a> - Presents final results</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/switch-mode">switch_mode</a> - Changes to a different mode for specialized tasks</li>
<li><a href="/RooVetGit/Roo-Code-Docs/blob/main/features/tools/new-task">new_task</a> - Creates a new subtask</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tool Calling Mechanism</h2><a id="user-content-tool-calling-mechanism" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tool Calling Mechanism" href="#tool-calling-mechanism"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">When Tools Are Called</h3><a id="user-content-when-tools-are-called" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: When Tools Are Called" href="#when-tools-are-called"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools are invoked under specific conditions:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Direct Task Requirements</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>When specific actions are needed to complete a task as decided by the LLM</li>
<li>In response to user requests</li>
<li>During automated workflows</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Mode-Based Availability</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Different modes enable different tool sets</li>
<li>Mode switches can trigger tool availability changes</li>
<li>Some tools are restricted to specific modes</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Context-Dependent Calls</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Based on the current state of the workspace</li>
<li>In response to system events</li>
<li>During error handling and recovery</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Decision Process</h3><a id="user-content-decision-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Decision Process" href="#decision-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The system uses a multi-step process to determine tool availability:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Mode Validation</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="isToolAllowedForMode(
    tool: string,
    modeSlug: string,
    customModes: ModeConfig[],
    toolRequirements?: Record&lt;string, boolean&gt;,
    toolParams?: Record&lt;string, any&gt;
)"><pre><span class="pl-en">isToolAllowedForMode</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">toolParams</span>?: <span class="pl-v">Record</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-smi">string</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-smi">any</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Requirement Checking</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>System capability verification</li>
<li>Resource availability</li>
<li>Permission validation</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Parameter Validation</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Required parameter presence</li>
<li>Parameter type checking</li>
<li>Value validation</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technical Implementation</h2><a id="user-content-technical-implementation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technical Implementation" href="#technical-implementation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tool Call Processing</h3><a id="user-content-tool-call-processing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tool Call Processing" href="#tool-call-processing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Initialization</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tool name and parameters are validated</li>
<li>Mode compatibility is checked</li>
<li>Requirements are verified</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Execution</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const toolCall = {
    type: &quot;tool_call&quot;,

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Result Handling</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Success/failure determination</li>
<li>Result formatting</li>
<li>Error handling</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Security and Permissions</h3><a id="user-content-security-and-permissions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security and Permissions" href="#security-and-permissions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Access Control</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>File system restrictions</li>
<li>Command execution limitations</li>
<li>Network access controls</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Validation Layers</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tool-specific validation</li>
<li>Mode-based restrictions</li>
<li>System-level checks</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mode Integration</h2><a id="user-content-mode-integration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mode Integration" href="#mode-integration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mode-Based Tool Access</h3><a id="user-content-mode-based-tool-access" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mode-Based Tool Access" href="#mode-based-tool-access"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tools are made available based on the current mode:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Code Mode</strong>: Full access to file system tools, code editing capabilities, command execution</li>
<li><strong>Ask Mode</strong>: Limited to reading tools, information gathering capabilities, no file system modifications</li>
<li><strong>Architect Mode</strong>: Design-focused tools, documentation capabilities, limited execution rights</li>
<li><strong>Custom Modes</strong>: Can be configured with specific tool access for specialized workflows</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mode Switching</h3><a id="user-content-mode-switching" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Mode Switching" href="#mode-switching"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Process</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Current mode state preservation</li>
<li>Tool availability updates</li>
<li>Context switching</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Impact on Tools</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tool set changes</li>
<li>Permission adjustments</li>
<li>Context preservation</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Best Practices</h2><a id="user-content-best-practices" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Best Practices" href="#best-practices"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tool Usage Guidelines</h3><a id="user-content-tool-usage-guidelines" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tool Usage Guidelines" href="#tool-usage-guidelines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Efficiency</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use the most specific tool for the task</li>
<li>Avoid redundant tool calls</li>
<li>Batch operations when possible</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Security</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Validate inputs before tool calls</li>
<li>Use minimum required permissions</li>
<li>Follow security best practices</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Error Handling</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Implement proper error checking</li>
<li>Provide meaningful error messages</li>
<li>Handle failures gracefully</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Patterns</h3><a id="user-content-common-patterns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Patterns" href="#common-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">

<li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Error Handling and Recovery</h2><a id="user-content-error-handling-and-recovery" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Error Handling and Recovery" href="#error-handling-and-recovery"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Error Types</h3><a id="user-content-error-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Error Types" href="#error-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Tool-Specific Errors</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Parameter validation failures</li>
<li>Execution errors</li>
<li>Resource access issues</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>System Errors</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Permission denied</li>
<li>Resource unavailable</li>
<li>Network failures</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Context Errors</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Invalid mode for tool</li>
<li>Missing requirements</li>
<li>State inconsistencies</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
